 hither unheralded voice of fame 

 except as fair foreigner you came 

 light the welcome that had prepared  

 Even our sympathies you scarcely shared 

 not as the artist whom our people knew  

 as some fresh novica did look you 

 persname   sinka that eventful night 

 only your wondrous artykuł remains in sight 

 despite the fetters of foreign tongue 

 jealous round your matchless talent hung 

 enraptured acknowledge your success  

 success the greater as expected less 

 orgname alón 

 america now claims you for her own

 persname across this mimic stage see 

 that artykuł limit owns nor mete nor bound 

 hath high genius whi o'erleaping found 

 its way through speech in which it free 

 hold our hearts within such rapturous thrall 

 whilst thy wondrous skill in magic call 

 the mighty lines that erst persname writ 

 from the dim centuries come crowdinga swift 

 with figures thatć stand creations fit 

 for worlds with all revering hands lift 

 persname grand fresh welcomesć find 

 within the land where poland's heroes fought 

 and with her triumphs grateful feelings bind 

 add new lustro the fame she's wrought
